function GetAvatarWorth(p168)

    local _MarketplaceService = u10:GetService('MarketplaceService')
    local _assets = _Players2:GetCharacterAppearanceInfoAsync(p168).assets
    local v172, v173, v174 = pairs(_assets)
    local v175 = 0

    while true do
        local v176

        v174, v176 = v172(v173, v174)

        if v174 == nil then
            break
        end

        local v177 = _MarketplaceService:GetProductInfo(v176.id, Enum.InfoType.Asset)

        if v177.IsForSale then
            v175 = v177.PriceInRobux + v175
        end
    end

    return v175
end

    end

    return v181
end

                            v207.Velocity = u35
                            v207.RotVelocity = u35
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
        end
    end
    if u197 and u65 ~= nil then
        local v208, v209, v210 = pairs(u65.Character:GetDescendants())

        while true do
            local v211

            v210, v211 = v208(v209, v210)

            if v210 == nil then
                break
            end
            if (u65.Character or u65 ~= nil) and v211:IsA('BasePart') then
                v211.CanCollide = false
                v211.Velocity = u35
                v211.RotVelocity = u35
            end
        end
    end
end

local function u215(p213)
    local v214 = math.floor(math.log(p213, 1000))

    return ('%.1f'):format(p213 / math.pow(10, v214 * 3)):gsub('%.?0+$', '') .. (u212[v214] or '')
end

function search_(p216, p217, p218)
    local v219 = p218 or 'Frame'
    local v220 = (p217 or 'nil'):lower()

    if v220 == '' then
        local v221 = p216:GetChildren()
        local v222, v223, v224 = pairs(v221)

        while true do
            local v225

            v224, v225 = v222(v223, v224)

            if v224 == nil then
                break
            end
            if v225:IsA(v219) then
                v225.Visible = true
            end
        end
    else
        local v226 = p216:GetChildren()
        local v227, v228, v229 = pairs(v226)

        while true do
            local v230

            v229, v230 = v227(v228, v229)

            if v229 == nil then
                break
            end
            if v230:IsA(v219) then
                local v231 = v230.Name:lower()

                if string.find(v231, v220) then
                    v230.Visible = true
                else
                    v230.Visible = false
                end
            end
        end
    end
end
function zeroGrav(p232)
    if not p232:FindFirstChild('BodyForce') then
        local _BodyForce = _new4('BodyForce')

        _BodyForce.Force = p232:GetMass() * Vector3.new(0, workspace.Gravity, 0)
        _BodyForce.Parent = p232
    end
end
function flungpart(p234)
    if not p234:FindFirstChild('BodyForce') then
        local _BodyForce2 = _new4('BodyForce')

        _BodyForce2.Force = p234.Position * 1000
        _BodyForce2.Parent = p234
    end
end

_cframe = {
    diff = function(p236, p237)
        return p236:Inverse() * p237
    end,
    toWorldPoint = function(p238)
        local v239 = _player.c():FindFirstChild('Right Arm') or _player.c():FindFirstChild('RightHand')
        local v240 = u45
        local v241 = v239.CFrame * v240:Inverse()

        if v239.Name == 'RightHand' then
            v241 = v239.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-90), 0, 0)
        end

        return _cframe.diff(v241, p238)
    end,
}

        end

        end
    end)
end
